375
376
377inline cFontPtr NEW_CFONT_CONSOLAS_32()
378{
379 cImage *img = new chai3d::cImage();
380 cLoadPNG(img, CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_BYTEARRAY));
381
382 cFontPtr font = cFont::create();
383 font->m_charset.m_base = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET_BASE;
384 font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
385 font->m_charset.m_width = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_WIDTH;
386 font->m_charset.m_height = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_HEIGHT;
387 font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET_PAGES;
388 for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
389 {
390 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i ];
391 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+1];
392 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+2];
393 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+3];
394 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+4];
395 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+5];
396 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+6];
397 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONT_CONSOLAS_32_CHARSET[8*i+7];
398 }
399 font->m_charset.preProcess();
400
401 font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<chai3d::cImage>(img));
402
403 return (font);
404}
